[2024-10-28 20:19:19] Generated objective: Implement a snippet that tests the automated construction of a basic copper plate production line by placing electric mining drills on a copper ore patch, connecting them via transport belts to stone furnaces, fueling the furnaces with coal from the automated mining system, and using inserters to load/unload materials. Verify the system successfully produces copper plates over time and interfaces correctly with the existing coal mining infrastructure.
[2024-10-28 20:19:42] # Find nearest copper ore patch
copper_patch = get_resource_patch(Resource.CopperOre, nearest(Resource.CopperOre))
assert copper_patch, "No copper ore patch found"

# Move to copper patch center
move_to(copper_patch.bounding_box.left_top)

# Place first mining drill
drill = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerMiningDrill, Direction.DOWN, copper_patch.bounding_box.left_top)
assert drill, "Failed to place first mining drill"

# Place furnace line
furnace = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.StoneFurnace, drill.position, Direction.DOWN, spacing=2)
assert furnace, "Failed to place first furnace"

current_furnace = furnace
for _ in range(3):
    current_furnace = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.StoneFurnace, current_furnace.position, Direction.RIGHT, spacing=1)
    assert current_furnace, "Failed to place furnace in line"

# Place input belt from drill to furnaces
input_belt_start = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.TransportBelt, drill.position, Direction.DOWN, spacing=0)
above_last_furnace = Position(x=current_furnace.position.x, y=current_furnace.position.y - 2.5)
input_belt = connect_entities(input_belt_start.position, above_last_furnace, Prototype.TransportBelt)
assert len(input_belt) > 0, "Failed to place input belt"

# Place more drills
current_drill = drill
for _ in range(3):
    new_drill = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.BurnerMiningDrill, current_drill.position, Direction.RIGHT, spacing=1)
    new_drill = rotate_entity(new_drill, Direction.DOWN)
    assert new_drill, "Failed to place additional drill"
    current_drill = new_drill

# Place coal input belt above drills
coal_belt_start = Position(x=drill.position.x, y=drill.position.y - 2)
coal_belt_end = Position(x=current_drill.position.x, y=drill.position.y - 2)
coal_belt = connect_entities(coal_belt_start, coal_belt_end, Prototype.TransportBelt)
assert len(coal_belt) > 0, "Failed to place coal belt"

# Place inserters for coal into drills
x = drill.position.x
while x <= current_drill.position.x:
    coal_inserter = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerInserter, Direction.DOWN, 
                                Position(x=x, y=coal_belt_start.y + 1))
    assert coal_inserter, "Failed to place coal inserter"
    x += 2

# Place inserters for copper ore into furnaces
x = furnace.position.x
while x <= current_furnace.position.x:
    ore_inserter = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerInserter, Direction.DOWN,
                               Position(x=x, y=furnace.position.y - 1))
    assert ore_inserter, "Failed to place ore inserter"
    x += 2

# Place output belt below furnaces
output_belt_start = Position(x=furnace.position.x, y=furnace.position.y + 2)
output_belt_end = Position(x=current_furnace.position.x, y=furnace.position.y + 2)
output_belt = connect_entities(output_belt_start, output_belt_end, Prototype.TransportBelt)
assert len(output_belt) > 0, "Failed to place output belt"

# Place output chest
output_chest = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.IronChest, output_belt[-1].position, Direction.RIGHT, spacing=1)
assert output_chest, "Failed to place output chest"

# Place output inserter
output_inserter = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerInserter, Direction.RIGHT,
                              Position(x=output_chest.position.x-1, y=output_chest.position.y))
assert output_inserter, "Failed to place output inserter"

# Connect to existing coal infrastructure and add initial fuel
coal_patch = get_resource_patch(Resource.Coal, nearest(Resource.Coal))
assert coal_patch, "No coal patch found"

move_to(coal_belt[0].position)
coal_placed = insert_item(Prototype.Coal, coal_belt[0], quantity=50)
assert coal_placed is not None, "Failed to place initial coal"

# Initial fueling of all entities
entities_to_fuel = []
x = drill.position.x
while x <= current_drill.position.x:
    entities_to_fuel.append(Position(x=x, y=drill.position.y))  # Drills
    entities_to_fuel.append(Position(x=x, y=coal_belt_start.y + 1))  # Coal inserters
    entities_to_fuel.append(Position(x=x, y=furnace.position.y))  # Furnaces
    entities_to_fuel.append(Position(x=x, y=furnace.position.y - 1))  # Ore inserters
    x += 2

for pos in entities_to_fuel:
    move_to(pos)
    entity = inspect_position(pos)
    if entity:
        insert_item(Prototype.Coal, entity, quantity=5)

# Verify setup after 30 seconds
sleep(30)
chest_contents = inspect_inventory(output_chest)
copper_plates = chest_contents.get(Prototype.CopperPlate, 0)
assert copper_plates > 0, "No copper plates produced after 30 seconds"
print(f"Success! {copper_plates} copper plates produced")

# Place input belt from drill to furnaces
input_belt_start = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.TransportBelt, drill.position, Direction.DOWN, spacing=0)
above_last_furnace = Position(x=current_furnace.position.x, y=current_furnace.position.y - 2.5)
input_belt = connect_entities(input_belt_start.position, above_last_furnace, Prototype.TransportBelt)
assert len(input_belt) > 0, "Failed to place input belt"

# Place more drills
current_drill = drill 
for _ in range(3):
    new_drill = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.BurnerMiningDrill, current_drill.position, Direction.RIGHT, spacing=1)
    assert new_drill, "Failed to place additional drill"
    rotate_entity(new_drill, Direction.DOWN)
    current_drill = new_drill

# Place coal input belt above drills
coal_belt_start = Position(x=drill.position.x, y=drill.position.y - 2)
coal_belt_end = Position(x=current_drill.position.x, y=drill.position.y - 2)
coal_belt = connect_entities(coal_belt_start, coal_belt_end, Prototype.TransportBelt)
assert len(coal_belt) > 0, "Failed to place coal belt"

# Place inserters for coal into drills
x = drill.position.x
while x <= current_drill.position.x:
    coal_inserter = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerInserter, Direction.DOWN, 
                                Position(x=x, y=coal_belt_start.y + 1))
    assert coal_inserter, "Failed to place coal inserter"
    x += 2

# Place inserters for copper ore into furnaces
x = furnace.position.x
while x <= current_furnace.position.x:
    ore_inserter = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerInserter, Direction.DOWN,
                               Position(x=x, y=furnace.position.y - 1))
    assert ore_inserter, "Failed to place ore inserter"
    x += 2

# Place output belt below furnaces
output_belt_start = Position(x=furnace.position.x, y=furnace.position.y + 2)
output_belt_end = Position(x=current_furnace.position.x + 2, y=furnace.position.y + 2)
output_belt = connect_entities(output_belt_start, output_belt_end, Prototype.TransportBelt)
assert len(output_belt) > 0, "Failed to place output belt"

# Place output inserters from furnaces
x = furnace.position.x
while x <= current_furnace.position.x:
    output_inserter = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerInserter, Direction.DOWN,
                                 Position(x=x, y=furnace.position.y + 1))
    assert output_inserter, "Failed to place output inserter"
    rotate_entity(output_inserter, Direction.DOWN)
    x += 2

# Place output chest at end of belt
move_to(output_belt[-1].position)
chest_pos = Position(x=output_belt[-1].position.x + 1, y=output_belt[-1].position.y)
output_chest = place_entity(Prototype.IronChest, Direction.UP, chest_pos)
assert output_chest, "Failed to place output chest"

# Connect to existing coal infrastructure and add initial fuel
coal_patch = get_resource_patch(Resource.Coal, nearest(Resource.Coal))
assert coal_patch, "No coal patch found"

move_to(coal_belt[0].position)
coal_placed = insert_item(Prototype.Coal, coal_belt[0], quantity=50)
assert coal_placed is not None, "Failed to place initial coal"

# Initial fueling of all entities
entities_to_fuel = []
x = drill.position.x
while x <= current_drill.position.x:
    entities_to_fuel.append(Position(x=x, y=drill.position.y))  # Drills
    entities_to_fuel.append(Position(x=x, y=coal_belt_start.y + 1))  # Coal inserters  
    entities_to_fuel.append(Position(x=x, y=furnace.position.y))  # Furnaces
    entities_to_fuel.append(Position(x=x, y=furnace.position.y - 1))  # Ore inserters
    x += 2

x = furnace.position.x
while x <= current_furnace.position.x:
    entities_to_fuel.append(Position(x=x, y=furnace.position.y + 1))  # Output inserters
    x += 2

for pos in entities_to_fuel:
    move_to(pos)
    entity = get_entity(Prototype.BurnerInserter, pos) or get_entity(Prototype.BurnerMiningDrill, pos) or get_entity(Prototype.StoneFurnace, pos)
    if entity:
        insert_item(Prototype.Coal, entity, quantity=5)

# Verify setup after 30 seconds
sleep(30)
chest_contents = inspect_inventory(output_chest)
copper_plates = chest_contents.get(Prototype.CopperPlate, 0)
assert copper_plates > 0, "No copper plates produced after 30 seconds"
print(f"Success! {copper_plates} copper plates produced")

copper_patch = get_resource_patch(Resource.CopperOre, nearest(Resource.CopperOre))

    current_furnace = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.StoneFurnace, current_furnace.position, Direction.RIGHT, spacing=2)
    assert current_furnace, "Failed to place furnace in line"

# Place input belt from drill to furnaces
belt_start = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.TransportBelt, drill.position, Direction.DOWN)
above_furnaces = Position(x=current_furnace.position.x + 1, y=furnace.position.y - 1)

# Place more drills
current_drill = drill
for _ in range(3):
    new_drill = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.BurnerMiningDrill, current_drill.position, Direction.RIGHT, spacing=2)
    assert new_drill, "Failed to place additional drill"
    rotate_entity(new_drill, Direction.DOWN)
    current_drill = new_drill

# Place coal input belt above drills
coal_belt_start = Position(x=drill.position.x, y=drill.position.y - 2)
coal_belt_end = Position(x=current_drill.position.x + 2, y=drill.position.y - 2)
coal_belt = connect_entities(coal_belt_start, coal_belt_end, Prototype.TransportBelt)
assert len(coal_belt) > 0, "Failed to place coal belt"

# Place inserters for coal into drills
x = drill.position.x
while x <= current_drill.position.x + 1:
    coal_inserter = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerInserter, Direction.DOWN,
                               Position(x=x, y=coal_belt_start.y + 1))
    assert coal_inserter, "Failed to place coal inserter"
    x += 2

# Place inserters for copper ore into furnaces
x = furnace.position.x
while x <= current_furnace.position.x + 1:
    ore_inserter = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerInserter, Direction.DOWN,
                               Position(x=x, y=furnace.position.y - 1))
    assert ore_inserter, "Failed to place ore inserter"
    x += 2

# Place output belt below furnaces  
output_belt_start = Position(x=furnace.position.x, y=furnace.position.y + 2)
output_belt_end = Position(x=current_furnace.position.x + 2, y=furnace.position.y + 2)
output_belt = connect_entities(output_belt_start, output_belt_end, Prototype.TransportBelt)
assert len(output_belt) > 0, "Failed to place output belt"

# Place output inserters from furnaces
x = furnace.position.x
while x <= current_furnace.position.x + 1:
    output_inserter = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerInserter, Direction.DOWN,
                                 Position(x=x, y=furnace.position.y + 1))
    assert output_inserter, "Failed to place output inserter"
    x += 2

# Place output chest at end of belt
chest_pos = Position(x=output_belt[-1].position.x + 1, y=output_belt[-1].position.y)
output_chest = place_entity(Prototype.IronChest, Direction.UP, chest_pos)
assert output_chest, "Failed to place output chest"

# Connect to coal infrastructure
coal_patch = get_resource_patch(Resource.Coal, nearest(Resource.Coal))
assert coal_patch, "No coal patch found"

# Initial fueling of all burner entities
for entity in get_entities({Prototype.BurnerMiningDrill, Prototype.BurnerInserter}):
    move_to(entity.position)
    coal_mined = harvest_resource(coal_patch.bounding_box.left_top, quantity=5)
    if coal_mined > 0:
        insert_item(Prototype.Coal, entity, quantity=5)

# Connect coal infrastructure
move_to(coal_belt[0].position)
connect_entities(coal_patch.bounding_box.center, coal_belt[0].position, Prototype.TransportBelt)

    current_furnace = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.StoneFurnace, current_furnace.position, Direction.RIGHT, spacing=2)
    assert current_furnace, "Failed to place furnace in line"

assert len(input_belt) > 0, "Failed to place input belt"

# Add more drills
current_drill = drill
for _ in range(3):
    new_drill = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.BurnerMiningDrill, current_drill.position, Direction.RIGHT, spacing=3)
    assert new_drill, "Failed to place additional drill"
    
    # Connect new drill to main belt using intermediate position
    intermediate_pos = Position(x=new_drill.drop_position.x, y=input_belt[0].position.y)
    connect_entities(new_drill.drop_position, intermediate_pos, Prototype.TransportBelt)
    connect_entities(intermediate_pos, input_belt[0].position, Prototype.TransportBelt)
    current_drill = new_drill

# Place coal input belt above drills
coal_belt_start = Position(x=drill.position.x, y=drill.position.y - 2)
coal_belt_end = Position(x=current_drill.position.x + 2, y=drill.position.y - 2)
coal_belt = connect_entities(coal_belt_start, coal_belt_end, Prototype.TransportBelt)
assert len(coal_belt) > 0, "Failed to place coal belt"

current_drill = drill
while current_drill:
    coal_inserter = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerInserter, Direction.DOWN,
                               Position(x=current_drill.position.x, y=current_drill.position.y - 1))
    assert coal_inserter, "Failed to place coal inserter"
    
    # Get next drill to the right
    entities = get_entities({Prototype.BurnerMiningDrill}, current_drill.position, 3)
    next_drill = None
    for entity in entities:
        if entity.position.x > current_drill.position.x:
            next_drill = entity
            break
    current_drill = next_drill

                               Position(x=current_furnace.position.x, y=current_furnace.position.y - 1))
    assert ore_inserter, "Failed to place ore inserter"

                               Position(x=current_furnace.position.x + 1, y=current_furnace.position.y))

            break

output_belt_end = Position(x=current_furnace.position.x + 2, y=furnace.position.y + 2)

    insert_item(Prototype.Coal, entity, quantity=5)

connect_entities(coal_source.position, coal_belt[0].position, Prototype.TransportBelt)
